[BACKTEST SUMMARY — JULY 3]
  Advance picks: 3/3 CORRECT ✅✅✅ (EGY, ARG, COL all correct)
  ML direction: 2/3 correct (EGY win ✅, ARG win ✅, COL win ✅ — all 3 correct actually)
  Total accuracy: 2/3 (under hit on 086, under hit on 088, MASSIVE over on 087)
  
  SYSTEMATIC BIASES IDENTIFIED:
  1. MODEL UNDERPRICES FAVORITES vs BOOK — consistently gives underdogs more credit
     - AUS +420 (model) vs +230 (book) — model too generous to AUS
     - ARG -139 (model) vs -714 (book) — model WAY too generous to CPV
     - COL +104 (model) vs -200 (book) — model too generous to GHA
  2. MODEL TOTAL TOO LOW for high-quality attacking teams (ARG scored 3 in AET)
  3. MODEL ADVANCE PROBABILITIES too conservative for heavy favorites
     - ARG: 73.8% model vs 96% implied by book (-3500)
     - COL: 67.2% model vs 85% implied by book (-575)
  4. LAMBDA VALUES appear deflated — tournament pace discount may be too aggressive

[RECALIBRATION TARGETS]
  1. Increase favorite strength multiplier (reduce underdog viability)
  2. Reduce tournament pace discount (currently too aggressive for KO stage)
  3. Increase lambda for top-tier teams (ARG, COL) in KO matches
  4. Adjust advance probability calculation — book is much sharper on advance lines
  5. Consider AET/penalty probability in total projections for KO matches

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
 MODEL ARCHITECTURE REFERENCE (from v17_jul3_engine.mjs)
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

[ENGINE] v17.0-KO26-RECALIBRATED-13MATCH
[SIMS] 1,000,000 Monte Carlo (Dixon-Coles adjusted Poisson)
[BACKTEST] 13 completed R32 matches (073-085)
[PROJECTION MATCHES] 086 (AUS/EGY), 087 (ARG/CPV), 088 (COL/GHA)

[LAMBDA COMPUTATION]
  Weighted composite of:
    xGW:  xG weight (0.25-0.50)
    xGOTW: xGOT weight (0.10-0.32)
    smW:  shot map xG weight (0.10-0.20)
    psW:  player stats xG weight (0.12-0.22)
    xAW:  xA weight (0.08-0.12)
    spW:  shot map xGOT weight (0.05-0.10)
    possW: possession adjustment (0.03-0.04)
    convW: conversion rate adjustment (0.05-0.06)
    rho:  Dixon-Coles correlation (-0.050 to -0.075)
    pace: tournament pace discount (0.022-0.045)
  
  Formula: lambda = (xGW*avgXG + xGOTW*avgXGOT + smW*avgSmXG + psW*avgPsXG + xAW*avgXA + spW*avgSmXGOT) * possAdj * convAdj * (1-pace)

[25 VARIATIONS]
  V1-V25 with different weight combinations
  Composite scorer: dir=45%, total=30%, spread=15%, btts=10%
  Winner variation used for final projections

[MARKET DERIVATION]
  Dixon-Coles joint probability matrix (MAX_G=9)
  ET model: Poisson(λ/3) for each team in extra time
  PKs: 50.5/49.5 split
  Spread line: 1.5 (fixed for all R32 matches)
  
[DATA SOURCES]
  wc2026_espn_expected_goals: homeXG, awayXG, homeXGOT, awayXGOT, homeXA, awayXA
  wc2026_espn_team_stats: possession, possessionAway
  wc2026_espn_match_stats: homeShots, awayShots, homeShotsOnGoal, awayShotsOnGoal
  wc2026_espn_player_stats: SUM(xG), SUM(xA), SUM(sog), SUM(xGOTC)
  wc2026_espn_shot_map: xg, xgot per team per match
  wc2026_matches: home_score, away_score, status
  wc2026_frozen_book_odds: all markets for backtest matches

[DB TABLES WRITTEN]
  wc2026_model_projections: full model output
  wc2026MatchOdds: model_* + lambda + proj_goals columns

[JULY 4 MATCHES TO MODEL]
  Need to query: what matches are on July 4?
  From ESPN API check earlier: no Jul 4 R32 matches found (760500/501 were Jul 3)
  Must check DB for Jul 4 schedule

[CRITICAL RECALIBRATION FINDINGS]
  1. Model systematically underprices favorites (gives underdogs too much credit)
  2. Tournament pace discount too aggressive (lambdas deflated)
  3. Advance probabilities too conservative vs book
  4. Total projections too low for high-quality attacking teams
  5. AET scoring not factored into total projections

[NEXT STEPS]
  Phase 3: Build v18 engine with recalibrated parameters
  - Reduce pace discount from 0.025-0.045 → 0.010-0.025
  - Add favorite strength multiplier (1.05-1.15x for top-tier teams)
  - Increase VSiN weight to 70-75% to pull totals closer to market
  - Add AET probability buffer to total projections for KO matches
  Phase 4: Run 25 variations with new parameters
  Phase 5: Select winner, lock parameters
  Phase 6: Generate Jul 4 projections

[ENGINE VERSION]: v17.0-KO26-RECALIBRATED-13MATCH
[N_SIMS]: 1,000,000

[MATH ENGINE]:
  - Dixon-Coles adjusted Poisson model
  - poissonPMF(k, lambda) — log-space computation
  - dcAdjust(x, y, lambda, mu, rho) — low-score correlation
  - runDCSim(lambdaH, lambdaA, rho, spreadLine) — full joint matrix MAX_G=9
  - ET model: Poisson(λ/3) for each team when draw
  - PKs: 50.5/49.5 split

[LAMBDA COMPUTATION]:
  buildGSRows(teamCode, xgAll, tsAll, msAll) — builds per-match feature rows
  computeLambda(teamCode, gsRows, psAll, smAll, v) — weighted composite:
    lambdaRaw = xGW*avgXG + xGOTW*avgXGOT + smW*avgSmXG + psW*avgPsXG + xAW*avgXA + spW*avgSmXGOT
    lambda = lambdaRaw * possAdj * (1 + convW*(convRate-0.35)) * (1 - pace)
    possAdj = 1 + possW * ((avgPoss-50)/50)

[25 VARIATIONS — WEIGHT STRUCTURE]:
  Each variation has: xGW, xGOTW, smW, psW, xAW, spW, possW, convW, rho, pace
  Example V1: xGW=0.35, xGOTW=0.20, smW=0.15, psW=0.15, xAW=0.10, spW=0.05, possW=0.03, convW=0.05, rho=0.060, pace=0.030

[BACKTEST GRADING — COMPOSITE SCORER]:
  composite = 45*(dirOk/n) + 30*(totalOk/n) + 15*(spreadOk/n) + 10*(bttsOk/n)
  - dirOk: model predicted winner matches actual (or draw with pD>0.2)
  - totalOk: over/under 2.5 correct
  - spreadOk: spread cover correct
  - bttsOk: both teams to score correct

[DB QUERIES — GROUP STAGE ONLY (matchRound='group-stage')]:
  - wc2026_espn_expected_goals: homeXG, awayXG, homeXGOT, awayXGOT, homeXA, awayXA
  - wc2026_espn_team_stats: possession, possessionAway
  - wc2026_espn_match_stats: homeShots, awayShots, homeShotsOnGoal, awayShotsOnGoal
  - wc2026_espn_player_stats: SUM(xG), SUM(xA), SUM(sog), SUM(xGOTC) GROUP BY match+team
  - wc2026_espn_shot_map: AVG(xg), AVG(xgot) GROUP BY match+team

[DB WRITES]:
  - wc2026_model_projections: full projection row per match
  - wc2026MatchOdds: model_* columns + lamba_home + lamba_away + model_projected_*_goals
